void setup()
{
  pinMode(13, INPUT);
  pinMode(12, INPUT);
  pinMode(10, OUTPUT);
  Serial.begin(9600);
}

void loop()
{
  if(digitalRead(13)== HIGH && digitalRead(12)== HIGH)
  {
    Serial.println("TANK FULL");
    digitalWrite(10,LOW);
  }
  if(digitalRead(13) == HIGH && digitalRead(12)==LOW)
  {
    Serial.println("TANK FULL (NOT REGULAR CASE)");
    digitalWrite(10,LOW);
  }
  if(digitalRead(13)==LOW && digitalRead(12)==HIGH)
  {
    Serial.println("NO change in status of motor");
    if(digitalRead(10) == LOW)
    {
      digitalWrite(10,LOW);
    }
    else{
      digitalWrite(10,HIGH);
    }
  }
  if(digitalRead(13) == LOW && digitalRead(12)== LOW)
  {
    Serial.println("NO WATER! SWITCH ON MOTOR");
    digitalWrite(10,HIGH);
  }
}

Yoga and Meditation
The objective of the course is to provide practical training in YOGA ASANAS with a sound theoretical base and

Kerala Mural Art and Painting
Mural painting is an offshoot of the devotional tradition of Kerala. A mural is any piece of artwork painted or applied
directly on a wall, ceiling or other large permanent surface. In the contemporary scenario Mural painting is not
restricted to the permanent structures and are being done even on canvas. Kerala mural paintings are the frescos
depicting mythology and legends, which are drawn on the walls of temples and churches in South India, principally
in Kerala. Ancient temples, churches and places in Kerala, South India, display an abounding tradition of mural
paintings mostly dating back between the 9th to 12th centuries when this form of art enjoyed Royal patronage.
Learning Mural painting through the theory and practice workshop is the objective of this course.
Course on Organic Farming and Sustainability
Organic farming is emerging as an important segment of human sustainability and healthy life. Haritamritamâ€™ is an
attempt to empower the youth with basic skills in tradition of organic farming and to revive the culture of growing
vegetables that one consumes, without using chemicals and pesticides. Growth of Agriculture through such positive
initiatives will go a long way in nation development. In Ammaâ€™s words â€œit is a big step in restoring the lost harmony
of natureâ€œ.
Benefits of Indian Medicinal Systems
Indian medicinal systems are one of the most ancient in the world. Even today society continues to derive enormous
benefits from the wealth of knowledge in Ayurveda of which is recognised as a viable and sustainable medicinal
tradition. This course will expose students to the fundamental principles and philosophy of Ayurveda and other Indian
medicinal traditions.
Traditional Fine Arts of India
India is home to one of the most diverse Art forms world over. The underlying philosophy of Indian life is â€˜Ãšnity in
Diversityâ€ and it has led to the most diverse expressions of culture in India. Most art forms of India are an expression
of devotion by the devotee towards the Lord and its influence in Indian life is very pervasive. This course will introduce
students to the deeper philosophical basis of Indian Art forms and attempt to provide a practical demonstration of the
continuing relevance of the Art.
Science of Worship in India
Indian mode of worship is unique among the world civilisations. Nowhere in the world has the philosophical idea of
reverence and worshipfulness for everything in this universe found universal acceptance as it in India. Indian religious
life even today is a practical demonstration of the potential for realisation of this profound truth. To see the allpervading consciousness in everything, including animate and inanimate, and constituting society to realise this truth
can be seen as the epitome of civilizational excellence. This course will discuss the principles and rationale behind
different modes of worship prevalent in India.

	    scanf("%d%d",&A,&B);
	    if(A%2!=0 && B%2!=0){
	        printf("%s\n","No");
	    }
	    else if(A==1||B==1){
	        printf("%s\n","No");
	    }
	    else{
	        printf("%s\n","Yes");
	    }
	}
	return 0;
}

		AuthorName = authorName;
	}

class book{

		private String name;
		private Author a;
		private double price;
		private int qty;
		public book() {};
		public book (String name, Author a, double price) { 
			this.name = name;
			this.a = a;
			this.price = price;
			
		}
		
		public book (String name, Author a, double price, int qty) { 
		this.name = name;
		this.a = a;
		this.price = price;
		this.qty = qty;
		}
		
		public void printdetails() {
			System.out.println("name of book is "+name+"and author name is "+a+"and price is "+ price + " and qty is "+qty);
		}
		
	



public String getName() {
			return name;
		}

		public void setName(String name) {
			this.name = name;
		}

		public double getPrice() {
			return price;
		}

		public void setPrice(double price) {
			this.price = price;
		}

		public int getQty() {
			return qty;
		}

		public void setQty(int qty) {
			this.qty = qty;
		}

}

09/11/22, 17:25 - Viswaa Ramasubramanian: package Assigmemt1;

import java.util.Scanner;

public class Qn30 {
    public static void main(String args[]){
        int a,s=0;
        Scanner in =new Scanner(System.in);
        a= in.nextInt();
        int d=a;

        for(int i=1;i<d;i++){
            if(d%i==0){
                s+=i;
            }
        }

        if(s==a){
            System.out.println("Perfect Number");
        }
        else{
            System.out.println("Not an Perfect Number");
        }
    }

}

import java.util.Scanner;

public class Qn30 {
    public static void main(String args[]){
        int a,s=0;
        Scanner in =new Scanner(System.in);
        a= in.nextInt();
        int d=a;

        for(int i=1;i<d;i++){
            if(d%i==0){
                s+=i;
            }
        }

        if(s==a){
            System.out.println("Perfect Number");
        }
        else{
            System.out.println("Not an Perfect Number");
        }
    }

}

public class Qn31 {

        Scanner in =new Scanner(System.in);

        }
        if(s==a){
            System.out.println("Armstrong");
        }
        else{
            System.out.println("Not an Armstrong");
        }
    }

}

import java.util.Scanner;

public class Qn33 {
    public static void main(String args[]){
        int n1=0,n2=1,n3,i,count;
        Scanner in = new Scanner(System.in);
        count=in.nextInt();
        if(count==1) {
            System.out.print(n1);
        }
        if(count>=2) {
            System.out.print(n1 + " " + n2);
        }
        for(i=2;i<count;++i)
        {
            n3=n1+n2;
            System.out.print(" "+n3);
            n1=n2;
            n2=n3;
        }
    }
}

import java.util.*;
public class Qn14 {
    public static void main(String args[]){
        Scanner sc=new Scanner(System.in);
        System.out.println("enter the side lengths: ");
        int a=sc.nextInt();
        int b=sc.nextInt();
        int c=sc.nextInt();
        if(a==b && b==c){
            System.out.println("Equilateral");
        }
        else if(a==b || b==c || a==c){
            System.out.println("Isosceles");
        }
        else{
            System.out.println("Scalene");
        }

    }
}

    static void find(char a)
    {
        if ((a >= 65 && a <= 90)
                || (a >= 97 && a <= 122))
            System.out.println(" Alphabet ");

            // CHECKING FOR DIGITS
        else if (a >= 48 && a <= 57)
            System.out.println(" Digit ");

        else
            System.out.println(" Special Character ");
    }

    // Driver Code
    public static void main(String[] args)
    {
        char a = '$';
        find(a);
    }
}

        System.out.println("Customer idno:" + custid);
        System.out.println("unit consumed:" + unit);
        if (unit <= 199)
            amt = unit * 1.2;
        else if (unit > 199 && unit < 400)
            amt = unit * 1.5;
        else if (unit >= 400 && unit < 600)
            amt = unit * 1.8 * 1.15;
        else if (unit >= 600)
            amt = 1.15 * (unit * 2);
        System.out.println("amount is " + amt);
    }
}

import java.util.*;
public class Qn26 {
    public static void main(String args[]){
        Scanner sc=new Scanner(System.in);
        System.out.println("Enter the value of n: ");
        int n= sc.nextInt();
        int c=0;
        int i=1;
        int s=0;
        System.out.println("odd numbers are: ");
        while(c<n){
            if(i%2==0){
                i++;
                continue;
            }
            else{
                System.out.print(i+" ");
                s+=i;
                c++;
                i++;
            }

        }
        System.out.println();
        System.out.println("the sum of odd numbers is "+s);


    }
}

class polynomial{
    private:
    int n,a[50],b[50];
    public:
    polynomial(){};
    polynomial(int x){

    }

17/11/22, 19:50 - Phoool Gobiiii  ğŸ“: #include <iostream>
using namespace std;

class Poly{
    private:
    int n = 5;
    int coeff[25]={};
    int pow[25] = {};

    public:
    Poly(){

    }
    Poly(int n, int a[], int b[]) {
        this->n=n;
        for (int i = 0; i < n; i++) {
            coeff[i] = a[i];
            pow[i] = b[i];
        }
    }
    void set_n(int n){
        this->n=n;
    }

    Poly operator *(Poly M){
        Poly N;
        N.set_n(this->n*M.n);
        int k = 0;
        for(int i = 0; i < this->n;i++) {
            for (int j = 0; j < M.n; j++) {
                N.coeff[k] = this->coeff[i] * M.coeff[j];
                N.pow[k] = this->pow[i] + M.pow[j];
                k++;
            }
        }
        return N;
    }

    void display(){
        cout << coeff[0] << " x^" << pow[0];
        for (int i = 1; i < n; i++) {
            cout << " + ";
            cout << coeff[i] << " x^" << pow[i];
        }
        cout << endl;
    }
};

int main() {
    int n1;
    cout << "Enter no of terms for 1st polynomial: ";
    cin >> n1;
    int coeff1[n1];
    int pow1[n1];
    for (int i = 0; i < n1; i ++) {
        cout << "Enter the coefficient for " <<i+1<<" term: ";
        cin >> coeff1[i];
        cout << "Enter the power for " <<i+1<<" term: ";
        cin >> pow1[i];
    }

    int n2;
    cout << "Enter no of terms for 2nd polynomial: ";
    cin >> n2;
    int coeff2[n2];
    int pow2[n2];
    for (int i = 0; i < n2; i ++) {
        cout << "Enter the coefficient for " <<i+1<<" term: ";
        cin >> coeff2[i];
        cout << "Enter the power for " <<i+1<<" term: ";
        cin >> pow2[i];
    }

    Poly A(n1, coeff1, pow1);
    A.display();
    cout << "-----" << endl;
    Poly B(n2, coeff2, pow2);
    B.display();
    cout << "-----" << endl;
    Poly R;
    R.set_n(n1*n2);

    R = A*B;
    R.display();

    return 0;
}

using namespace std;
class sailboat
{
private:
    string mname;
    int length;
    int width;
    int draught;

public:
    void setinfo(string name, int l, int w, int d)
    {
        mname = name;
        length = l;
        width = w;
        draught = d;
    }
    void writeinfo()
    {
        cout << mname << " " << length << " " << width << " " << draught << endl;
    }
    int operator>(sailboat m)
    {
        int v = 0;
        if (length > m.length)
        {
            v = 1;
        }
        else if (length == m.length && width > m.width)
        {
            v = 1;
        }
        return v;
    }
};
int main()
{
    sailboat s[3], t;
    int length, width, draught;
    string name;
    for (int i = 0; i < 3; i++)
    {
        cout << "Enter values: " << endl;
        cin >> name >> length >> width >> draught;
        s[i].setinfo(name, length, width, draught);
    }
    int i, j;
    for (int i = 0; i < 2; i++)
    {
        for (int j = 0; j < 2 - i; j++)
        {
            if (s[j] > s[j + 1])
            {
                t = s[j];
                s[j] = s[j + 1];
                s[j + 1] = t;
            }
        }
    }
    for (int i = 0; i < 3; i++)
    {
        s[i].writeinfo();
    }
}

using namespace std;

class num{
	int n;
	
	public:
		void set(int a){
			n=a;
		}
		void set(char a){
			cout<<"Enter a number: ";
			cin>>n;
		}
		int get(){
			return n;
		}
};
class perfect: public num{
	
	public:
		int checkPerfect(){
			int sum=0;
			for (int i=1;i<get();i++){
				if(get()%i==0){
					sum+=i;
				}
			}
			if(sum==get()){
				return 1;
			}
			else{
				return 0;
			}
		}
};
int main(){
	perfect obj;
	obj.set('a');
	(obj.checkPerfect())?cout<<"Perfect":cout<<"Not Perfect";
}

import java.util.Scanner;

public class Menu {
    String[] foodName = new String[5];
    String[] drinkName = new String[5];
    double[] foodPrice = new double[5];
    double[] drinkPrice= new double[5];

    public void order(){
        Scanner sc = new Scanner(System.in);
        System.out.print("Enter the no of food items: ");
        int foodN = sc.nextInt();
        System.out.print("Enter the no of drinks: ");
        int drinkN = sc.nextInt();

        for (int i = 0; i < foodN; i++) {
            System.out.print("Enter the food name: ");
//            foodName[i] = "";
            sc.nextLine();
            foodName[i] = sc.nextLine();
            System.out.print("Enter the food price: ");
            foodPrice[i] = sc.nextDouble();
        }

        for (int i = 0; i < drinkN; i++) {
            System.out.print("Enter the drink name: ");
//            drinkName[i] = "";
            sc.nextLine();
            drinkName[i] = sc.nextLine();
            System.out.print("Enter the drink price: ");
            drinkPrice[i] = sc.nextDouble();
        }
    }
}
21/11/22, 11:54 - Phoool Gobiiii  ğŸ“: package P1_Practice;

import java.util.Scanner;

public class Order {
    double tax;
    double total;
    String paymentMethod;
    Scanner sc = new Scanner(System.in);
    public void calculateBill(Menu m1){
        double foodSum = 0;
        double drinkSum = 0;
        for (int i = 0; i < (m1.foodPrice.length); i++) {
            foodSum += m1.foodPrice[i];
        }
        for (int i = 0; i < (m1.drinkPrice.length); i++) {
            drinkSum += m1.drinkPrice[i];
        }
        total += ((foodSum + 0.035*foodSum) + (drinkSum + 0.048*drinkSum));
        tax += 0.035*foodSum + 0.048*drinkSum;
    }


    public void pay(){
        System.out.print("Enter payment method: ");
        paymentMethod = sc.next();
    }

    public void display(Menu m1){
        System.out.println();
        System.out.println("Receipt");
        for (int i = 0; i < (m1.foodName.length); i++) {
            if (m1.foodName[i] != null) {
                System.out.println(m1.foodName[i] + "\t" + m1.foodPrice[i]);
            }
        }
        for (int i = 0; i < (m1.drinkName.length); i++) {
            if (m1.drinkName[i] != null) {
                System.out.println(m1.drinkName[i] + "\t" + m1.drinkPrice[i]);
            }
        }
        System.out.println();
        System.out.println("Tax = " + tax);
        System.out.println("Total = " + total);
        System.out.println("Payment mode: " + paymentMethod);
    }
}

class Amount():
    def __init__(self,amount=None):
        self.amount = amount
    def calculate(self):
        d = {}
        rupee,paisa=self.amount.split(".")
        rupee=int(rupee)
        paisa=int(paisa)
        d["rupees"]=rupee
        print(rupee,paisa)
        nt=rupee//1000
        rupee=rupee%1000
        nh=rupee//100
        rupee=rupee%100
        nf=rupee//50
        rupee=rupee%50
        ntw=rupee//20
        rupee=rupee%20
        nten=rupee//10
        rupee=rupee%10
        nfive=rupee//5
        rupee=rupee%5
        ntwo=rupee//2
        rupee=rupee%2
        nones=rupee//1
        rupee=rupee%1
        d["thousands"]=nt
        d["Hundreds"]=nh
        d["Fifties"]=nf
        d["Twenties"]=ntw
        d["Tens"]=nten
        d["Fives"]=nfive
        d["Twos"]=ntwo
        d["Ones"]=nones
        d["Paisa"]=paisa
        print(nt,nh,nf,ntw,nten,nfive,ntwo,nones)
        return d
    def __add__(self, other):
        d={}
        rupee1, paisa1 = self.amount.split(".")
        rupee1=int(rupee1)
        paisa1 = int(paisa1)
        rupee2,paisa2 = other.amount.split(".")
        rupee2 = int(rupee2)
        paisa2 = int(paisa2)
        if(paisa1+paisa2<100):
            d["rupees"]=rupee1+rupee2
            d["Paisa"]=paisa1+paisa2
        else:
            d["rupees"]=rupee1+rupee2+1
            d["Paisa"]=(paisa1+paisa2)-100
        return d
    def __lt__(self, other):
        amt1=float(self.amount)
        amt2=float(other.amount)
        if(amt1<amt2):
            return 1
        elif(amt1>amt2):
            return -1
        else:
            return 0
    def __sub__(self, other):
        d={}
        rupee1, paisa1 = self.amount.split(".")
        rupee1 = int(rupee1)
        paisa1 = int(paisa1)
        rupee2, paisa2 = other.amount.split(".")
        rupee2 = int(rupee2)
        paisa2 = int(paisa2)
        if(paisa1-paisa2>=0):
            d["rupees"] = rupee1 - rupee2
            d["Paisa"] = paisa1 - paisa2
        elif(paisa1-paisa2<0):
            d["rupees"] = rupee1 - rupee2-1
            d["Paisa"] = 100+(paisa1 - paisa2)
        return d

class Amount:
    def __init__(self,rupees=0,paise=0):
        self.rupees=rupees
        self.paise=paise
    def count1000(self):
        thousandCount=(self.rupees//1000)
        remainingRupees=self.rupees%1000
        self.rupees=remainingRupees
        return thousandCount
    def count100(self):
        hundredCount = (self.rupees // 100)
        remainingRupees = self.rupees % 100
        self.rupees = remainingRupees
        return hundredCount
    def count50(self):
        hundredCount = (self.rupees // 50)
        remainingRupees = self.rupees % 50
        self.rupees = remainingRupees
        return hundredCount
    def count20(self):
        hundredCount = (self.rupees // 20)
        remainingRupees = self.rupees % 20
        self.rupees = remainingRupees
        return hundredCount
    def count10(self):
        hundredCount = (self.rupees // 10)
        remainingRupees = self.rupees % 10
        self.rupees = remainingRupees
        return hundredCount
    def count5(self):
        hundredCount = (self.rupees // 5)
        remainingRupees = self.rupees % 5
        self.rupees = remainingRupees
        return hundredCount
    def count2(self):
        hundredCount = (self.rupees //2)
        remainingRupees = self.rupees % 2
        self.rupees = remainingRupees
        return hundredCount
    def count1(self):
        hundredCount = (self.rupees // 1)
        remainingRupees = self.rupees % 1
        self.rupees = remainingRupees
        return hundredCount
    def __add__(self, other):
        o=Amount()
        o.paise=self.paise+other.paise
        o.rupees=self.rupees+other.rupees
        o.rupees+=o.paise//100
        o.paise=100-o.paise%100
        return o
    def __sub__(self, other):
        o = Amount()
        if(self.rupees>other.rupees):
            o.rupees = self.rupees - other.rupees
            o.paise = self.paise - other.paise
            if(o.paise<0):
                o.paise=(o.paise%100)
                o.rupees=o.rupees-1
        elif(other.rupees>self.rupees):
            o.rupees = other.rupees - self.rupees
            o.paise = other.paise - self.paise
            if (o.paise < 0):
                o.paise = (o.paise % 100)
                o.rupees = o.rupees - 1
        else:
            if(self.paise>other.paise):
                o.rupees = other.rupees - self.rupees
                o.paise = self.paise - other.paise
            elif(other.paise>self.paise):
                o.rupees = other.rupees - self.rupees
                o.paise = other.paise - self.paise
            else:
                o.paise=0
                o.rupees=0
        return o
    def getRupee(self):
        return self.rupees
    def getPaise(self):
        return self.paise
rupees=int(input("Rupees for obj1:"))
paise=int(input("Paise for obj1:"))
amt=Amount(rupees,paise)
rupees1=int(input("Rupees for obj2:"))
paise1=int(input("Paise for obj2:"))
amt1=Amount(rupees1,paise1)

07/12/22, 19:15 - Sooorrrr ğŸ“: import java.util.Scanner;
public class circle1 extends Shape1 {

    private int radius;

    public void setRadius(int radius) {
        this.radius = radius;
    }
    public int getRadius() {
        return radius;
    }
    @Override
    public double area() {

        return 3.14*radius*radius;

    }

    @Override
    public double perimeter() {
        return 3.14*2*radius;
    }
    public static void main(String args[]){
        int radius;
        System.out.println("Enter radius");
        Scanner sc = new Scanner(System.in);
        radius = sc.nextInt();
        circle1 c1=new circle1();
        c1.setRadius(radius);
        System.out.println(c1.getRadius());
        System.out.println(c1.area());
        System.out.println(c1.perimeter());
    }

}

08/12/22, 12:53 - Sooorrrr ğŸ“: package Pack;

public class Multithreading extends Thread{
    private int n;
    public Multithreading(int n){
        this.n=n;
    }
    @Override
    public void run() {
        for(int i = 1; i <4; i++) {
            System.out.println(i+" from thread"+n);
            if(n==3){
                throw  new RuntimeException();
            }
            try {
                Thread.sleep(500);
            }
            catch(InterruptedException e){
            }
        }
    }
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        for(int i = 0; i <5;i++){

            Multithreading mt = new Multithreading(i);
            mt.start();
        }
    }

}
08/12/22, 12:56 - Sooorrrr ğŸ“: package Pack;

public class Multithreading implements Runnable{
    private int n;
    public Multithreading(int n){
        this.n=n;
    }
    @Override
    public void run() {
        for(int i = 1; i <4; i++) {
            System.out.println(i+" from thread"+n);
       
            try {
                Thread.sleep(500);
            }
            catch(InterruptedException e){
            }
        }
    }
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        for(int i = 0; i <5;i++){

            Multithreading mt = new Multithreading(i);
            Thread mythread = new Thread(mt);
            mythread.start();
        }
    }

}

Inheritance - "IS-A" Relationship
-Overriding - runtime poly
-Code reusability 

Generalization
Generalization is the process of extracting shared characteristics from two or more classes, and combining them into a generalized superclass. Shared characteristics can be attributes, associations, or methods.

Specialization
Find an existing class that already implements some of the desired chars.
- Inherit it to a new class and add unique properties

Subtyping (Extensions)
-derived class is behaviourally compatible with the base class
-Behaviourally compatible means that base class can be replaced by the derived class

class sub-name extends sup-name
{

}

Rules for inherited method:
-> Methods declared public in a superclass also must be public in sub
-> Methods declared protected in a superclass must be protected/ public in sub. NOT PRIVATE
-> Methods declared in private ain't inherited at all.

TYPES of Inheritance:
->Single - single baseclass <= single derived class
->Mutilevel - single base class+ single derived class + multiple intermediate base classes
->Hierarchical - one base class + multiple subclass

->Multiple
->Hybrid

*In java multiple and hybrid can be achieved only via INTERFACE

for every class in java there exist super class: java.lang.Object

Dynamic Method Dispatch
->assign the base class reference to a child class obj
eg: <parentclass_name> OBJ =  new <childclass_name>();

Visibility

public> protected> default> private

Polymorphism:
we can create functions or reference variables which behaves differently

Types of POLY:
-Coercion :- Implicit type conversion
-Overloading :- a single identifier denotes several abstractions

- Subtype:-
-> a type can serve as another type's subtype
->Widening
  -aka upcasting
  -The conversion of a subtype to one of its supertypes is called widening. 
->Narrowing
  -aka downcasting
  -The conversioning of a supertype to one of its subtypes is called narrowing
  -Narrowing requires a proper explicit cast

Upcasting:

REFERENCE <parentclass> and OBJECT <childclass>
eg:
  class A{}
  class B extends A{}
  A a=new B();//upcasting
-> ACCESS: Parents own method and childs overridden methods

BINDING
â€¢ Connecting a method call to the method body is known as binding.
â€¢ There are two types of binding
  â€“ Static Binding (also known as Early Binding):Object type resolved by compiler - private, final or static method
  â€“ Dynamic Binding (also known as Late Binding):Object type resolved at runtime  -

DOWNCASTING:
eg:
Parent p = new Child(); //first upcast
Child c =(Child) p;     // use the upcasted obj to downcast


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Process is a Code, data, and stack
â€“ Usually (but not always) has its own address space (An address space is a range of valid addresses in memory that are available for a program or process.)

Process creation:
->Parent process creates children processes, which, in turn create other processes, forming a tree of processes
->process identified and managed via a process identifier (pid)

Resource sharing options
â€“ Parent and children share all resources
â€“ Children share subset of parentâ€™s resources
â€“ Parent and child share no resources

Execution options
â€“ Parent and children execute concurrently
â€“ Parent waits until children terminate

â€¢ Conditions that terminate processes can be
â€“ Voluntary : Normal exit, Error exit
â€“ Involuntary : Fatal error, Killed by another process

Processes in the OS
- 2 layers
- Lowest layer: handles interrupts/scheduling
- Above layer: sequential processes
		-> Processes tracked in the process table (Process Control Block)
		-> Each process has a process table entry

Thread:
-Independent stream of instructions
-Basic unit of CPU Utilization
-DS used is Thread Control Block

-Contains:
 ->Thread ID
 ->A register set (inc. Program Counter PC)
 ->An execution Stack 
 
-A thread shares :
		->Code, data and heap section
		-> OS resourcse (open files and signals)
 with its sibling threads

-no memory protection

USES:
- Allow a single application to do many things at once: multitasking
â€“ Simpler programming model
â€“ Less waiting

-faster to create or destroy

Types:
User level:
+ No need for kernel support
- May be slower than kernel threads
- Harder to do non-blocking I/O

Kernel-level :
+ More flexible scheduling
+ Non-blocking I/O
- Not portable

Thread Scheduling 
-Allows to:
-> assign priorities to processes
->CPU to select processes with higher priority

â€“ Policy set by what priorities are assigned to processes

Userlevel:

-Kernel picks a process to run next
-Run-time system (at user level) schedules threads
  â€“> Run each thread for less than process quantum
  â€“> Example: processes get 40ms each, threads get 10ms each

Kernel level:

-Kernel schedules each thread
  â€“> No restrictions on ordering
  â€“> May be more difficult for each process to specify priorities

Thread Scheduler in JAVA:
-A part of the JVM
-no guarantee that which runnable thread will be chosen to run by the thread scheduler.
-Only one thread at a time can run in a single process.

Preemptive scheduling vs time slicing
â€“ Preemptive scheduling, the highest priority task executes until it enters the waiting or dead states or a higher priority task comes into existence.
â€“ Time slicing, a task executes for a predefined slice of time and then re-enters the pool of ready tasks. The scheduler then determines which task should execute next, based on priority and other factors.


â€¢Each thread have a priority
â€¢ Priorities are represented by a number between 1 and 10

â€¢ 3 constants defined in Thread class:
â€“ public static int MIN_PRIORITY - 1
â€“ public static int NORM_PRIORITY - 5
â€“ public static int MAX_PRIORITY - 10

States of thread in java

â€“ new: just created but not started
â€“ runnable: created, started, and able to run
â€“ blocked: created and started but unable to run because it is waiting for some event to occur
â€“ dead: thread has finished or been stopped

Portability issues (JVM)
in Linux:
â€“ A thread runs to completion or until a higher priority thread
becomes ready
â€“ Preemption occurs (processor is given to the higher-priority
thread)

On Win32:
â€“ Threads are timesliced
  -> Thread given quantum of time to execute
  -> Processor then switched to any threads of equal priority
â€“ Preemption occurs with higher and equal priority threads

Challenges in programming for multi-core chips:
â€¢ Identifying tasks - Examining applications to find activities that can be performed concurrently.
â€¢ Balance - Finding tasks to run concurrently that provide equal value. I.e. don't waste a thread on trivial tasks.
â€¢ Data splitting - To prevent the threads from interfering with one another.
â€¢ Data dependency - If one task is dependent upon the results of another, then the tasks need to be synchronized to assure access in the proper order.
â€¢ Testing and debugging - Inherently more difficult in parallel processing situations, as the race conditions become much more complex and difficult to identify.


Creating threads in java:
-user-level threads which connects to JVM kernel-level threads 
(pthreads in UNIX or Win32 threads in windows.)

-2 Ways:
â€“ Option 1: Extend the Thread class and override the public run method
â€“ Option 2: Implement a runnable interface with a public run method


OPTION 1: EXTEND
```
package practice;

class PrintNumbers1 extends Thread {
	public void printNumbers() {
		for (int i = 0; i < 9; i++) {
			System.out.println(Thread.currentThread().getId() + ": " + i);
		}
	}

	@Override
	public void run() {
		printNumbers();
// the super doesn't anything,
// but just for the courtesy and good practice
		super.run();
	}

public class Thread2 {
	public static void main(String[] args) {
		System.out.println("Main ThreadId: " +
		Thread.currentThread().getId());
		for(int i=0; i<3; i++) {
		new PrintNumbers1().start(); // don't call run! (if you want a separate thread)
		}
		}

}

```


OPTION 2: RUNNABLE

```
package practice;

import java.io.*;

class PrintNumbers implements Runnable {
	public void printNumbers() {
		for (int i = 0; i < 9; i++) {
			System.out.println(Thread.currentThread().getId() + ": " + i);
		}
	}

	@Override
	public void run() {
		printNumbers();
	}
}

public class Inheritance1 {

	public static void main(String[] args) {
		//

		System.out.println("Main ThreadId: " + Thread.currentThread().getId());
		for (int i = 0; i < 3; i++) {
			Thread t1=new Thread(new PrintNumbers());
			t1.start(); // don't call run!
	}

	}
}
```




Thread related methods:
â€“ Constructors
	â€¢ Thread() - Creates a thread with an auto-numbered name of format Thread-1, Thread-2...
	â€¢ Thread( threadName ) - Creates a thread with name

â€“ run
	â€¢ Does â€œworkâ€ of a thread â€“ What does this mean?
	â€¢ Can be overridden in subclass of Thread or in Runnable object (more on interface Runnable elsewhere)

â€“ start
	â€¢ Launches thread, then returns to caller
	â€¢ Calls run
	â€¢ Error to call start twice for same thread

The Thread Class:

+Thread() -> Creates a default thread
+Thread(task: Runnable) -> Creates thread for a specified task 
+start(): void -> Starts the thread that causes the run() method to be invoked by the JVM
+isAlive(): boolean ->Tests whether the thread is currently running.
+setPriority(p: int): void ->Sets priority p (ranging from 1 to 10) for this thread
+join(): void -> Waits for this thread to finish
+sleep(millis: long): void ->Puts the runnable object to sleep for a specified time in milliseconds
+yield(): void ->Causes this thread to temporarily pause and allow other threads to execute.
+interrupt(): void ->Interrupts this thread

Advantage of Using Runnable
â€¢ remember - can only extend one class
â€¢ implementing runnable allows class to extend something else

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Abstract Classes
â€¢ An Abstract class is a conceptual
class.
â€¢ An Abstract class cannot be
instantiated â€“ objects cannot be
created.
â€¢ Abstract classes provides a common
root for a group of classes, nicely tied
together in a package:

Syntax
public abstract class <ClassName>

â€¢ A class with one or more abstract methods is
automatically abstract and it cannot be
instantiated.
â€¢ A class declared abstract, even with no abstract
methods in it.
â€¢ A subclass of an abstract class can be
instantiated if it overrides all abstract methods and
implements them.
â€¢ A subclass that does not implement all of the
superclass abstract methods in it, then the
subclass cannot be instantiated.


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Packages
â€¢ Packages are containers for classes that are used to keep the class namespace compartmentalized.

â€¢ simply include a package command as the first statement in a Java source file.
â€¢ Any classes declared within that file will belong to the specified package.
â€¢ The package statement defines a name space in which classes are stored.
â€¢ If you omit the package statement, the class names are put into the default package, which has no name.
â€¢ While the default package is fine for short, sample programs, it is inadequate for real applications. 

â€¢ You can create a hierarchy of
packages.
Syntax
package pkg1[.pkg2[.pkg3]];

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Interface: - public/ static/ final
->conceptual entity similar to a Abstract class.
â€“> But can contain only constants (final variables) and abstract method (no implementation)

â€¢ One class can implement many interfaces
â€¢ One interface can be implemented by many
classes â€“ But can contain only constants (final variables) and
abstract method (no implementation) - Different from
Abstract classes


*Normally, in order for a method to be called from one class to another, both classes need to be present at compile time
functionality gets pushed up higher and higher in the class hierarchy so that the mechanisms will be available to more and more subclasses. 
Can be avoided by interface.
INTERFACES designed to support dynamic method resolution at run time. 

â€“ They disconnect the definition of a method or set of methods from the inheritance hierarchy.
â€“ Since interfaces are in a different hierarchy from classes, it is possible for classes that are unrelated in terms of the class hierarchy to implement the same interface. 


final variable

Modifier static final dataType variableName = value; //initialized final variable
Or
modifier static final dataType variableName; //blank final variable

*We must initialize the blank final variable in constructor or in a a block of the class otherwise it will throw a compilation error

Drawbacks of Constants in Java
â€¢ Constants holding primitive types do not change value once initialized.
â€¢ Constants holding derived data types (array, object references) do not allow change in the memory reference.
â€“ However the data values in the memory can be changed.
â€“ So, the state of the object can be changed but not the reference
=>final Variable in Java â‰  Const in C/C++

â€¢ When a class implements an interface that inherits
another interface, it must provide implementations
for all methods defined within the interface
inheritance chain. 

Marker interface:
-â€¢ An empty interface is called a â€œMarker Interfaceâ€ or â€œTaggingInterfaceâ€
â€“ java.lang.Cloneable and java.io.Seria lizable are examples of marker interfaces.

import random
class TicTacToe:
    def _init_(self):
        self.board = []
    def create_board(self):
        for i in range(3):
            row = []
            for j in range(3):
                row.append('-')
            self.board.append(row)
    def get_random_first_player(self):
        return random.randint(0, 1)
    def fix_spot(self, row, col, player):
        self.board[row][col] = player
    def is_player_win(self, player):
        win = None
        n = len(self.board)
        # checking rows
        for i in range(n):
            win = True
            for j in range(n):
                if self.board[i][j] != player:
                    win = False
                    break
            if win:
                return win
        # checking columns
        for i in range(n):
            win = True
            for j in range(n):
                if self.board[j][i] != player:
                    win = False
                    break
            if win:
                return win
        # checking diagonals
        win = True
        for i in range(n):
            if self.board[i][i] != player:
                win = False
                break
        if win:
            return win
        win = True
        for i in range(n):
            if self.board[i][n - 1 - i] != player:
                win = False
                break
        if win:
            return win
        return False
        for row in self.board:
            for item in row:
                if item == '-':
                    return False
        return True
    def is_board_filled(self):
        for row in self.board:
            for item in row:
                if item == '-':
                    return False
        return True
    def swap_player_turn(self, player):
        return 'X' if player == 'O' else 'O'
    def show_board(self):
        for row in self.board:
            for item in row:
                print(item, end=" ")
            print()
    def start(self):
        self.create_board()
        player = 'X' if self.get_random_first_player() == 1 else 'O'
        while True:
            print(f"Player {player} turn")
            self.show_board()
            # taking user input
            row, col = list(map(int, input("Enter row and column numbers to fix spot: ").split()))
            print()
            # fixing the spot
            self.fix_spot(row - 1, col - 1, player)
            # checking whether current player is won or not
            if self.is_player_win(player):
                print(f"Player {player} wins the game!")
                break
            # checking whether the game is draw or not
            if self.is_board_filled():
                print("Match Draw!")
                break
            # swapping the turn
            player = self.swap_player_turn(player)
        # showing the final view of board
        print()
        self.show_board()
# starting the game
tic_tac_toe = TicTacToe()
tic_tac_toe.start()





def get_divisors(N):
    a=[]
    b=[]
    count=0
    for i in N:
        divisors=[]
        for j in range(1,i+1):
            if i%j==0:
                divisors.append(j)
            else:
                continue
        a.append([i,divisors,len(divisors)])
    print(a)
    max=-1
    for i in a:
        if i[2]>max:
            max=i[2]
            b=i
    return b

open=['[','{','(']
close=[']','}',')']
def check(s):
    l=[]
    for i in s:
        if i in open:
            l.append(i)
        elif i in close:
            p=close.index(i)
            if len(l)>0 and open[p]==l[-1]:
                l.pop()
            else:
                return 'unbalanced'
    if len(l)==0:
        return 'balanced'
    else:
        return 'unbalanced'
        
s=input()
t=input()
u=input()
v=input()
print(check(s))
print(check(t))
print(check(u))
print(check(v))




def sum(l,num):
    x=[]
    for i in range(len(l)):
        for j in range(i+1,len(l)):
            if l[i]+l[j]==num:
                x.append([l[i],l[j]])
    return x           
        
l=[1,2,3,4,5,6,7,8,9]
print(sum(l,10))





def triangle(n):
     
    
    k = n - 1
 
    
    for i in range(0, n):
     
        
        for j in range(0, k):
            print(end=" ")
     
       
        k = k - 1
     
    
        for j in range(0, i+1):
         
            
            print("* ", end="")
     
        
        print("\r")

def validation(str1):
    stack = []
    parenDict = {'(': ')', '{': '}', '[': ']'}
    for p in str1:
        if p in parenDict:
            stack.append(p)
        elif p.isalnum():
            continue
        elif p in "!@#$%^&*_-=+:;><,./?|":
            continue
        elif len(stack) == 0 or parenDict[stack.pop()] != p:
            return False
    return len(stack) == 0
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
num = [1,4,5,9,10,40,50,90,100,400,500,900,1000]
sym = ['I' , 'IV' , 'V' , 'IX' , 'X' , 'XL' , 'L' , 'XC' , 'C' , 'CD' , 'D' , 'CM' ,'M']
n = int(input())

int sum(int n){
	int s=0;
	int i=0;
	/*@
		loop invariant s==i*(i+1);
		loop invariant 0<=i<=(2*n)+1;
		loop assigns s,i;
		loop variant (2*n)-i;
	*/
	while(i<=(2*n)){
		i+=2;
		s+=i;		
	}
	return s;
}

int sum(int n){

    /*@
        loop invariant s==i*(i+1);
        loop invariant 0<=i && i<=n+1;
        loop assigns s,i;
        loop variant 2*n-i;

29/12/22, 15:59 - Sanjuuu ğŸ“: /*@ 
requires units>=0;
ensures \result>=0;
assigns \nothing;
behavior a:
	assumes units<=50;
	ensures \result == units * 0.50;
behavior b:
	assumes units<=150;
	ensures \result == 25 + (units - 50) * 0.75;
behavior c:
	assumes units<=250;
	ensures \result == 100 + (units - 150) * 1.20;
behavior d:
	assumes units>250;
	ensures \result == 220 + (units - 250) * 1.50;
complete behaviors a,b,c,d;
	
*/

float eb(int units)
{
	float amount=0;

	
    if (units <= 50)
    {
        amount = units * 0.50;
    }
    else if (units <= 150)
    {
        amount = 25 + (units - 50) * 0.75;
    }
    else if (units <= 250)
    {
        amount = 100 + (units - 150) * 1.20;
    }
    else
    {
        amount = 220 + (units - 250) * 1.50;
    }

    return amount;
    
}

03/01/23, 09:22 - Sanjuuu ğŸ“: #include <stdio.h>
/*@ requires \valid(a+(0..n-1));
	requires n>0;
	ensures \forall integer i,j; 0<=i<=j<=n-1 ==> a[i]<=a[j];
*/

void BubbleSort(int *a, int n){
	int i,j,temp;
	/*@ 
		loop invariant \forall integer p,q; i<=p<=q<=n-1 ==> a[p]<=a[q];
		loop invariant \forall integer p,q; 0<=p<i+1==q<=n-1 ==> a[p]<=a[q];
		loop invariant 0<=i<n;
		loop assigns i, j, temp, a[0..n-1];
		loop variant i;
	*/
	for(i=n-1;i>0;i--){
		/*@ loop invariant 0<=j<=i<n;
			 loop invariant \forall integer k; 0<=k<=j ==> a[k] <= a[j];
			 loop invariant \forall integer p, q; 0<=p<i+1==q<=n-1 ==> a[p]<=a[q];
			 loop assigns j,temp,a[0..i];
			 loop variant i-j;
		 */
		 for(j=0; j<i; j++) {
			 if (a[j] > a[j+1]) {
				 temp = a[j];
				 a[j] = a[j+1];
				 a[j+1] = temp;
			 }
		 }
		
	}

}

    stack<int> s;
    while (!q.empty()) {
        s.push(q.front());
        q.pop();
    }
    while (!s.empty()) {
        q.push(s.top());
        s.pop();
    }

    }

}

stack <int> rev(stack <int> s){
    stack <int> s3;
    while(!s.empty()){
        s3.push(s.top());
        s.pop();
    }
    return s3;
}
int main(){
    stack <int> s1;
    s1.push(5);
    s1.push(4);
    s1.push(3);
    stack <int> s2;
    s2=rev(s1);
    s2.pop();
    s1=rev(s2);
    cout<<endl;
    while(!s1.empty()){
        cout<<s1.top()<<" ";
        s1.pop();
    }
}

05/01/23, 14:01 - Viswaa Ramasubramanian: #include <unordered_set>
#include <vector>

void removeDuplicates(std::vector<int>& vec) {
  std::unordered_set<int> seen;
  std::vector<int> result;

  for (int x : vec) {
    if (seen.count(x) == 0) {
      // Element has not been seen before, add it to the result vector
      result.push_back(x);
      seen.insert(x);
    }
  }

  vec = result;  // Overwrite the original vector with the result vector
}
05/01/23, 14:04 - Viswaa Ramasubramanian: #include <list>

void removeDuplicates(std::list<int>& lst) {
  std::list<int> seen;

  for (auto it = lst.begin(); it != lst.end(); ) {
    if (std::find(seen.begin(), seen.end(), *it) != seen.end()) {
      // Element has been seen before, remove it from the list
      it = lst.erase(it);
    } else {
      // Element is new, add it to the seen list
      seen.push_back(*it);
      ++it;
    }
  }
}

06/01/23, 08:40 - Viswaa Ramasubramanian: /*@ requires base_salary > 0;
   ensures \result == base_salary * 1.2 + base_salary * 0.8 || \result == base_salary * 1.25 + base_salary * 0.9 || \result == base_salary * 1.3 + base_salary * 0.95;
   behavior low:
     assumes base_salary <= 10000 && base_salary>0;
     ensures \result == base_salary * 1.2 + base_salary * 0.8;
   behavior medium:
     assumes base_salary > 10000 && base_salary <= 20000;
     ensures \result == base_salary * 1.25 + base_salary * 0.9;
   behavior high:
     assumes base_salary > 20000;
     ensures \result == base_salary * 1.3 + base_salary * 0.95;
  */
float calc_gross_salary(float base_salary) {
  float hra, da;
  if (base_salary <= 10000 && base_salary>0) {
    hra = base_salary * 0.2;
    da = base_salary * 0.8;
    return base_salary + hra + da;
  } else if (base_salary <= 20000 && base_salary>10000) {
    hra = base_salary * 0.25;
    da = base_salary * 0.9;
    return base_salary + hra + da;
  } else if(base_salary >20000) {
    hra = base_salary * 0.3;
    da = base_salary * 0.95;
    return base_salary + hra + da;
  }
  else{
    return false;
  }
  
}
void main(){
    float base_salary=15000;
    calc_gross_salary(base_salary);


}

06/01/23, 12:55 - Araviiii ğŸ“: /*@
	requires n>0;
	ensures \result==(n*n);

*/

int sum(int n)
{
	int s=0;
	int i=0;
	/*@
		loop invariant s==(i*i);
		loop invariant 0<=i<=(n);
		loop assigns s,i;
		loop variant (n)-i;
	*/
	
	while(i<n)
	{
		i=i+1;
		s=s+(2*i)-1;
	}
	return s;
}

int main()
{
	int a=4;
	sum(a);
}

15/01/23, 23:21 - Sanjuuu ğŸ“: class Node:
    def _init_(self, data):
        self.data = data
        self.next = None
        self.prev = None

class DoublyLinkedList:
    def _init_(self):
        self.head = None

    def append(self, data):
        new_node = Node(data)
        if self.head is None:
            self.head = new_node
        else:
            current = self.head
            while current.next:
                current = current.next
            current.next = new_node
            new_node.prev = current

    def prepend(self, data):
        new_node = Node(data)
        if self.head is None:
            self.head = new_node
        else:
            new_node.next = self.head
            self.head.prev = new_node
            self.head = new_node

    def delete(self, data):
        current = self.head
        if current is not None:
            if current.data == data:
                self.head = current.next
                current.next.prev = None
            else:
                while current.next is not None:
                    if current.data == data:
                        break
                    current = current.next
                if current.next is not None:
                    current.prev.next = current.next
                    current.next.prev = current.prev
                else:
                    if current.data == data:
                        current.prev.next = None

    def print_list(self):
        current = self.head
        while current:
            print(current.data)
            current = current.next

15/01/23, 23:31 - Sanjuuu ğŸ“: class Stack():
    def __init__(self):
        self.items = []

    def isempty(self):
        if len(self.items) == 0:
            return True
        else:
            return False

    def push(self, item):
        self.items.append(item)

    def pop(self):
        if not self.isempty():
            return self.items.pop()
        else:
            return None

    def peek(self):
        if not self.isempty:
            return self.items[-1]
        else:
            return None

    def size(self):
        return len(self.items)


class Queue:
    def __init__(self):
        self.queue = []

    def enqueue(self, item):
        self.queue.append(item)

    def dequeue(self):
        if len(self.queue) < 1:
            return None
        return self.queue.pop(0)

    def size(self):
        return len(self.queue)

    def reverse(self):
        temp = Stack()
        temp2 = self
        while temp2.size != 0:
            temp.push(temp2.dequeue())
        while not temp.isempty():
            temp2.enqueue(temp.pop())
        return temp2

The password is set through another input (p1, p2, p3, p4, p5) and the user entered value is input through the line (u1, u2, u3, u4, u5).

One way to implement this logic circuit is by using XOR gates and an AND gate. XOR gates are used to compare each bit of the password to the corresponding bit of the user input. If all the bits of the user input match the corresponding bits of the password, the XOR gates will output 0, indicating that the user input matches the password. The output of these XOR gates will be connected to an AND gate, which will determine whether the user input matches the password. If the user input matches the password, the AND gate will output a 1, indicating that the data (b1, b2, b3, b4) can be sent to the display (y1, y2, y3, y4).

First, we need to establish the ASCII codes for the letters â€˜aâ€™, â€˜bâ€™, and â€˜câ€™ for the last 2 bits. These are 01, 10, and 11 respectively in binary.

To compare the last two bits of the 8-bit input to the ASCII codes of â€˜aâ€™, â€˜bâ€™, and â€˜câ€™, we can use a 2:1 multiplexer (MUX) to select the last two bits of the 8-bit input.
Then we can use a series of 2 comparators, one for each bit of the selected two bits of the input.
Each comparator compares one bit of the input to the corresponding bit of the ASCII code for â€˜aâ€™, â€˜bâ€™, or â€˜câ€™.
If both comparators output a 1, it means that the input matches the ASCII code for that letter.

The outputs of the comparators for â€˜aâ€™, â€˜bâ€™, and â€˜câ€™ can be connected to AND gates.
If the input matches the ASCII code for â€˜aâ€™, the output of the AND gate for â€˜aâ€™ will be 1, which can be used to assert the output a_recd.
Similarly, if the input matches the ASCII code for â€˜bâ€™, the output of the AND gate for â€˜bâ€™ will be 1, which can be used to assert the output b_recd.
And if the input matches the ASCII code for â€˜câ€™, the output of the AND gate for â€˜câ€™ will be 1, which can be used to assert the output c_recd.

17/01/23, 12:47 - Viswaa Ramasubramanian: class node:
    def __init__(self, data):
        self.data = data
        self.next = None


class sll:
    def __init__(self):
        self.head = None

    def printl(self):
        n = self.head

        if n is None:
            print("the linked list is empty")
        else:
            while n is not None:
                print(n.data)
                n = n.next

    #size of sll
    def size(self):
        n=self.head
        size=0
        if n is None:
            return size
        else:
            while n is not None:
                size=size+1
                n=n.next
            return size



    def adde(self, data):#add end
        new = node(data)
        if self.head is None:
            self.head = new
        else:
            n = self.head
            while n.next is not None:
                n = n.next
            n.next = new

    def addb(self, data):#add beginning
        newn = node(data)
        newn.next = self.head
        self.head = newn

    def addat(self,data,p):#add after element p
        new = node(data)
        if self.head is None:
            self.head = new
        else:
            n = self.head
            while n.data is not p:
                n = n.next
            new.next = n.next
            n.next = new

    # insert at a particular position or replace
    def rep(self, p, e):
        new = node(e)
        n = self.head
        prev = self.head
        if self.head is None:
            self.head = new
        else:
            i = 0
            while (i < p):
                n = n.next
                i = i + 1
            while prev.next is not n:
                prev = prev.next
        prev.next = new
        new.next = n.next

    def rep2(self, p, e):
        new = node(e)

        if self.head is None:
            self.head = new
        else:

                n = n.next
                i = i + 1

    def addbefnode(self, p, e):
        new = node(e)

    #delete after a node
    def delafter(self,p):

        else:
            if(p==self.size()):

    def swap(self,p,q):

        p2=self.head
        if self.head is None:
            print("empty")

                i=i+1
            while(j<q):
                p2=p2.next
                j=j+1
            t1=p1.data
            t2=p2.data
            self.rep(p,t2)
            self.rep(q,t1)

                i=i+1
            while(j<q):
                p2=p2.next
                j=j+1
            p1.data,p2.data=p2.data,p1.data

class sll:
    def __init__(self):
        self.head = None

    def printl(self):
        n = self.head

        if n is None:
            print("the linked list is empty")
        else:
            while n is not None:
                print(n.data)
                n = n.next

    #size of sll
    def size(self):
        n=self.head
        size=0
        if n is None:
            return size
        else:
            while n is not None:
                size=size+1
                n=n.next
            return size

    #first element
    def first(self):
        if self.head is None:
            print("the list is empty")
        else:
            return self.head.data

    #last element
    def last(self):
        if self.head is None:
            print("the list is empty")
        else:
            n=self.head
            while n.next is not None:
                n=n.next
            return n.data

    def isfirst(self,p):
        if self.head is None:
            print("the list is empty")
        else:
            return self.head.data==p;

    def islast(self,p):
        if self.head is None:
            print("the list is empty")
        else:
            n=self.head
            while n.next is not None:
                n=n.next
            return n.data==p

    def getnode(self,p):
        if self.head is None:
            print("the list is empty")
        else:
            n=self.head
            count=0
            while n.data is not p and n.next is not None:
                n=n.next
                count=count+1
            if count==self.size()-1:
                return -1
            else:
                return count


    def adde(self, data):#add end
        new = node(data)
        if self.head is None:
            self.head = new
        else:
            n = self.head
            while n.next is not None:
                n = n.next
            n.next = new

    def addb(self, data):#add beginning
        newn = node(data)
        newn.next = self.head
        self.head = newn

    def addat(self,data,p):#add after element p

        else:

                n = n.next
            new.next = n.next
            n.next = new

    # insert at a particular position or replace
    def rep(self, p, e):
        new = node(e)

        prev = self.head
        if self.head is None:
            self.head = new
        else:
            i = 0

                n = n.next
                i = i + 1
            while prev.next is not n:
                prev = prev.next
        prev.next = new
        new.next = n.next

    def deleteAfter(self, l):#(based on element)
        currentNode = self.head
        while currentNode.data != l:
            currentNode = currentNode.next
        if (not currentNode.next is None):
            currentNode.next = currentNode.next.next
        else:
            print("No element found!")


    def deleteBefore(self, l):#based on element
        currentNode = self.head
        if (currentNode.data == l):
            print("No element found!")
        else:
            while currentNode.next.next.data != l:
                currentNode = currentNode.next
            currentNode.next = currentNode.next.next

    #swap elements of two nodes using replace
    def swap(self,p,q):
        p1=self.head
        p2=self.head
        if self.head is None:
            print("empty")

            i,j=0,0

                i=i+1
            while(j<q):
                p2=p2.next
                j=j+1
            t1=p1.data
            t2=p2.data
            self.rep(p,t2)
            self.rep(q,t1)

17/01/23, 13:48 - Sooorrrr ğŸ“: class Stack:
    def __init__(self):
        self.items = []

    def isEmpty(self):
        if len(self.items) == 0:
            return True
        else:
            return False

    def printstack(self):
        for i in range(-1, -len(self.items)-1,-1):
            print(self.items[i])

    def push(self, item):
        self.items.append(item)

    def pop(self):
        if not self.isEmpty():
            return self.items.pop()
        else:
            return None

    def top(self):
        if not self.isEmpty():
            return self.items[-1]
        else:
            return None

    def size(self):
        return len(self.items)

st.push(1)
st.push(2)

class Queue:
    def __init__(self):
        self.queue = []

    def printqueue(self):
        print(self.queue)

    def enqueue(self, item):
        self.queue.append(item)

    def dequeue(self):
        if len(self.queue) < 1:
            return None
        return self.queue.pop(0)

    def size(self):
        return len(self.queue)

    def reverse(self):
        temp = Stack()
        temp2 = self
        while temp2.size != 0:
            temp.push(temp2.dequeue())
        while not temp.isEmpty():
            temp2.enqueue(temp.pop())
        return temp2

q=Queue()
q.enqueue(1)
q.enqueue(2)
q.printqueue()

#include <bits/stdc++.h>
#include <math.h>
using namespace std;
stack <int> rev(stack <int> s){
    stack <int> s3;
    while(!s.empty()){
        s3.push(s.top());
        s.pop();
    }
    return s3;
}
int main(){
    stack <int> s1;
    s1.push(5);
    s1.push(4);
    s1.push(3);
    stack <int> s2;
    s2=rev(s1);
    s2.pop();
    s1=rev(s2);
    cout<<endl;
    while(!s1.empty()){
        cout<<s1.top()<<" ";
        s1.pop();
    }
}
17/01/23, 17:10 - Sooorrrr ğŸ“: #include <iostream>
using namespace std;
class Matrix{
    private:
    int n;
    int m;
    int arr[100][100]={};
    public:
    Matrix(){}
    Matrix(int n,int m){
        this->n=n;
        this->m=m;
    }
    void getmat(){
        for(int i=0;i<n;i++){
            for(int j=0;j<m;j++){
                cout<<"Enter an element";
                cin>>arr[i][j];
            }
        }
    }
    void print(){
        for(int i=0;i<n;i++){
            for(int j=0;j<m;j++){
                cout<<arr[i][j]<<endl;
            }
        }
    }
    Matrix operator +(Matrix obj){
        Matrix temp;
        for(int i=0;i<n;i++){
            for(int j=0;j<m;j++){
                temp.arr[i][j]=arr[i][j]+obj.arr[i][j];
            }
        }
        temp.n=n;
        temp.m=m;
        return temp;
    }
    Matrix operator *(Matrix obj){
        Matrix t;
        for(int i=0;i<n;i++){
            for(int j=0;j<m;j++){
                for(int k=0;k<m;k++){
                    t.arr[i][j]+=arr[i][k]*obj.arr[k][j];
                }
            }
        }
        t.n=n;
        t.m=m;
        return t;
    }
};
int main(){
    int n,m;
    cout<<"Enter the value of n"<<endl;
    cin>>n;
    cout<<"Enter the value of m"<<endl;
    cin>>m;
    Matrix mat1(n,m);
    mat1.getmat();
    mat1.print();
    cout<<"Enter the values of next matrix : "<<endl;
    Matrix mat2(n,m);
    mat2.getmat();
    mat2.print();
    cout<<"Values of sum matrix : "<<endl;
    Matrix mat3;
    mat3=mat1+mat2;
    mat3.print();
    cout<<"Values of multi matrix : "<<endl;
    Matrix mat4;
    mat4=mat1*mat2;
    mat4.print();
}

            this->b = b;
        }
        T getMax();
};

template<class T>
T myPair<T>::getMax(){
    T returnVal;
    returnVal=a>b?a:b;
    return returnVal;
}

int main(){
    myPair<int> obj(100,75);
    cout<<obj.getMax();
}

#include <list>
#include <math.h>
using namespace std;
class Hash{
    int Bucket;
    list<int> *container;
    public :
    Hash(int Bucket){
        this->Bucket = Bucket;
        list <int> container[Bucket];
    }
    int hashFunction(int x) {
        return (x % Bucket);
    }
    void insertitem(int key){
        int index=hashFunction(key);
        container[index].push_back(key);
    }
    void removeitem(int key){
        int index=hashFunction(key);
        list <int>:: iterator it;
        for(it=container[index].begin(); it!=container[index].end();it++){
            if(*it==key){
                break;
            }
        }
        if(it!=container[index].end()){
            container[index].erase(it);
        }
    }
    void display(){
        for(int i=0; i<Bucket;i++){
            cout << i <<" ";
            for(auto items:container[i]){
                cout<<"----->"<<items;

            }
            cout<<endl;
        }
    }
};

int main(){
    int a[]={15,11,27,8,12};
    int n=sizeof(a)/sizeof(a[0]);
    Hash h(7);
    for(int i=0;i<n;i++){
        h.insertitem(a[i]);
    }
    h.removeitem(12);
    h.display();
    return 0;
}

using namespace std;

class Hash{

    private:
    int Bucket;
    list<int> *container;
    
    public :
    Hash(int Bucket){
        this->Bucket = Bucket;
        container=new list<int> [Bucket];
    }

    int hashFunction(int x) {
        return (x % Bucket);
    }

    void insertitem(int key){
        int index=hashFunction(key);
        container[index].push_back(key);
    }

    void removeitem(int key){
        int index=hashFunction(key);
        list <int>:: iterator it;
        for(it=container[index].begin(); it!=container[index].end();it++){
            if(*it==key){
                break;
            }
        }
        if(it!=container[index].end()){
            container[index].erase(it);
        }
    }

    void display(){
        for(int i=0; i<Bucket;i++){
            cout << i <<" ";
            for(auto items:container[i]){
                cout<<"----->"<<items;

            }
            cout<<endl;
        }
    }
};

17/01/23, 21:47 - Gannu: #include <iostream>
#include <stack>
using namespace std;
void dis(stack <int> s){
    while(!s.empty()){
        cout<<s.top()<<" ";
        s.pop();
    }
    cout<<endl; 
}
void rev(stack <int> s){
    stack <int> sn;
    while(!s.empty()){
        sn.push(s.top());
        s.pop();
    }
    while(!sn.empty()){
        cout<<sn.top()<<" ";
        sn.pop();
    }
}
int main()
{
    stack <int> s1;
    s1.push(1);
    s1.push(2);
    s1.push(3);
    dis(s1);
    stack <int> s2;
    while(!(s1.size()==1)){
        s2.push(s1.top());
        s1.pop();
    }
    rev(s2);

}
17/01/23, 22:02 - Viswaa Ramasubramanian: stack <int> rev_stack(stack <int> s){
    stack <int> r;
    while (!s.empty()){
        r.push(s.top());
        s.pop();

    }
    
    return r;
}

stack <int> queue_del(stack <int> s){
    s = rev_stack(s);
    s.pop();
    s = rev_stack(s);
    return s;
}

void display_queue(stack <int> s){
    s = rev_stack(s);
    while(!s.empty()){
        cout << s.top()<< " ";
        s.pop();
    }

}

int main(){
    stack <int> s;
    s.push(1);
    s.push(2);
    s.push(3);
    s.push(4);
    s.push(5);
    s.push(6);

    s = queue_del(s);
    display_queue(s);
    cout << endl;
    s = queue_del(s);
    display_queue(s);

    s.push(7);

class adder{
    private:
    int x;
    int y;
    public:
    adder(){
        x=0;
        y=0;
    }
    adder(int u, int v){
        x=u;
        y=v;
    }
    adder operator + (adder obj){
        adder c;
        c.x=x+obj.x;
        c.y=y+obj.y;
        return c;
    }
    adder operator - (adder obj){
        adder c;
        c.x=x-obj.x;
        c.y=y-obj.y;
        return c;
    }
    void operator +=(adder obj){
        x=x+2*obj.x;
        y=y+2*obj.y;
    }
    void operator -=(adder obj){
        x=x-2*obj.x;
        y=y-2*obj.y;
    }
    void display(){
        cout<<x<<" ";
        cout<<y<<endl;
    }
    void operator -(){
        x=x-2;
        y=y-2;
    }
    void operator +(){
        x=x+2;
        y=y+2;

    }
};

17/01/23, 22:30 - Sooorrrr ğŸ“: #include <iostream>
#include <queue>
using namespace std;
 
// driver code
int main()
{
    int arr[6] = { 10, 2, 4, 8, 6, 9 };
 
    // defining priority queue
    priority_queue<int> pq;
 
    // printing array
    cout << "Array: ";
    for (auto i : arr) {
        cout << i << ' ';
    }
    cout << endl;
    // pushing array sequentially one by one
    for (int i = 0; i < 6; i++) {
        pq.push(arr[i]);
    }
 
    // printing priority queue
    cout << "Priority Queue: ";
    while (!pq.empty()) {
        cout << pq.top() << ' ';
        pq.pop();
    }
 
    return 0;
}

    int n;

class armstrong:public number{
    protected:
    int rem=0,m=0;
    public:
    void fun(){
        int t=n;
        while(n!=0){
        rem=n%10;
        n=n/10;
        m+=rem*rem*rem;
        }
        if(m==t){
            cout<<"It is an armstrong number"<<endl;
        }
        else{
            cout<<"It is not an armstrong number"<<endl;
        }
    }
};
class perfect:public number{
    public:
    void per(){
        int sum=0;
        for(int i=1;i<n;i++){
            if(n%i==0){
                sum+=i;
            }
        }
        if(sum==n){
            cout<<"It is a perfect number"<<endl;
        }
        else{
            cout<<"It is not a perfect number"<<endl;
        }
    }
};
int main(){
    int x;
    cout<<"Enter a value:"<<endl;
    cin>>x;
    armstrong num;
    num.setnumber(x);
    num.check();
    num.fun();
    perfect num1;
    num1.setnumber(x);
    num1.check();
    num1.per();

}
17/01/23, 22:34 - Gannu: // C++ program to demonstrate the use of priority_queue
#include <iostream>
#include <queue>
using namespace std;

// driver code
int main()
{
	int arr[6] = { 10, 2, 4, 8, 6, 9 };

	// defining priority queue
	priority_queue<int> pq;

	// printing array
	cout << "Array: ";
	for (auto i : arr) {
		cout << i << ' ';
	}
	cout << endl;
	// pushing array sequentially one by one
	for (int i = 0; i < 6; i++) {
		pq.push(arr[i]);
	}

	// printing priority queue
	cout << "Priority Queue: ";
	while (!pq.empty()) {
		cout << pq.top() << ' ';
		pq.pop();
	}

	return 0;
}

17/01/23, 22:34 - Sooorrrr ğŸ“: #include <iostream>
using namespace std;
class Matrix{
    private:
    int n;
    int m;
    int arr[100][100]={};
    public:
    Matrix(){}
    Matrix(int n,int m){
        this->n=n;
        this->m=m;
    }
    void getmat(){
        for(int i=0;i<n;i++){
            for(int j=0;j<m;j++){
                cout<<"Enter an element";
                cin>>arr[i][j];
            }
        }
    }
    void print(){
        for(int i=0;i<n;i++){
            for(int j=0;j<m;j++){
                cout<<arr[i][j]<<endl;
            }
        }
    }
    Matrix operator +(Matrix obj){
        Matrix temp;
        for(int i=0;i<n;i++){
            for(int j=0;j<m;j++){
                temp.arr[i][j]=arr[i][j]+obj.arr[i][j];
            }
        }
        temp.n=n;
        temp.m=m;
        return temp;
    }
    Matrix operator *(Matrix obj){
        Matrix t;
        for(int i=0;i<n;i++){
            for(int j=0;j<m;j++){
                for(int k=0;k<m;k++){
                    t.arr[i][j]+=arr[i][k]*obj.arr[k][j];
                }
            }
        }
        t.n=n;
        t.m=m;
        return t;
    }
};
int main(){
    int n,m;
    cout<<"Enter the value of n"<<endl;
    cin>>n;
    cout<<"Enter the value of m"<<endl;
    cin>>m;
    Matrix mat1(n,m);
    mat1.getmat();
    mat1.print();
    cout<<"Enter the values of next matrix : "<<endl;
    Matrix mat2(n,m);
    mat2.getmat();
    mat2.print();
    cout<<"Values of sum matrix : "<<endl;
    Matrix mat3;
    mat3=mat1+mat2;
    mat3.print();
    cout<<"Values of multi matrix : "<<endl;
    Matrix mat4;
    mat4=mat1*mat2;
    mat4.print();
}

    polynomial(){};
    polynomial(int n){
        this->n=n;
    }
    void set(int x, int y[10],int z[10]){
        n=x;
        for(int i=0; i<n; i++){
            arr[i]=y[i];
            brr[i]=z[i];
        }
    }
    polynomial operator *(polynomial m){
        polynomial temp;
        int k;
        k=0;

        for(int i=0; i<n; i++){
            for(int j=0;j<m.n; j++){
                temp.arr[k]=arr[i]*m.arr[j];
                temp.brr[k]=brr[i]+m.brr[j];
                k++;
            }
        }
        temp.n=this->n * m.n;
        return temp;
    }
    void display(){
        cout<<n<<endl;
        cout<<arr[0]<<"x^"<<brr[0];
        for(int i=1; i<n;i++){
            cout<<" + ";
            cout<<arr[i]<<"x^"<<brr[i];

class palindrome{
    private:
    int n;
    public:
    palindrome(int n){
        this->n=n;
    }
    void check(){
        int t=n;
        int rem,res;
        while(n!=0){
            rem=n%10;
            res=res*10 + rem;
            n=n/10;
        }
        if(res==t){
            cout<<"It is a palindrome "<<endl;
        }
        else{
            cout<<"It is not a palindrome "<<endl;
        }
    }
};

17/01/23, 22:40 - Gannu: // C++ program to demonstrate the use of priority_queue
#include <iostream>
#include <queue>
using namespace std;

// driver code
int main()
{
	int arr[6] = { 10, 2, 4, 8, 6, 9 };

	// defining priority queue
	priority_queue<int,vector<int>,greater <int>> pq;

	// printing array
	cout << "Array: ";
	for (auto i : arr) {
		cout << i << ' ';
	}
	cout << endl;
	// pushing array sequentially one by one
	for (int i = 0; i < 6; i++) {
		pq.push(arr[i]);
	}

	// printing priority queue
	cout << "Priority Queue: ";
	while (!pq.empty()) {
		cout << pq.top() << ' ';
		pq.pop();
	}

	return 0;
}

class add{
    int a ;
    public:
    add(){
        a=0;
    }
    friend add operator ++(add &obj);
    friend add operator ++(add &obj,int);
    friend add operator --(add &obj);
    friend add operator --(add &obj ,int);
    void display(){
        cout<<"A = "<<a<<endl;
    }
};

add operator ++(add &obj){
    obj.a+=1;
    return obj;
}
add operator ++(add &obj,int){
    add temp;
    temp.a=obj.a++;
    return temp;
}
add operator --(add &obj){
    obj.a-=1;
    return obj;
}
add operator --(add &obj,int){ 
    add temp ;
    temp.a = obj.a --;
    return temp;
}

int main(){
    add a1, a2 , a3;
    for(int i=0;i<3;i++){
        cout<<"Post increment:"<<endl;
        a1++.display();(++a2).display();a3++.display();
    }
    for (int i=0;i<3;i++){
        cout<<"preincrement:"<<endl;
        a1--.display();(--a2).display();a3--.display();
    }
}

18/01/23, 09:05 - Harecharan CSE E Amrita CBE: #include <iostream>
using namespace std;

class Fraction {
    int num, den;

public:
    Fraction(int n, int d) : num(n), den(d) {}

    // Overloading the + operator
    Fraction operator+(const Fraction &f2) {
        int n = num * f2.den + den * f2.num;
        int d = den * f2.den;
        return Fraction(n, d);
    }

    // Overloading the - operator
    Fraction operator-(const Fraction &f2) {
        int n = num * f2.den - den * f2.num;
        int d = den * f2.den;
        return Fraction(n, d);
    }

    // Overloading the * operator
    Fraction operator*(const Fraction &f2) {
        int n = num * f2.num;
        int d = den * f2.den;
        return Fraction(n, d);
    }

    // Overloading the / operator
    Fraction operator/(const Fraction &f2) {
        int n = num * f2.den;
        int d = den * f2.num;
        return Fraction(n, d);
    }

    // Overloading the < operator
    bool operator<(const Fraction &f2) {
        return (num * f2.den < den * f2.num);
    }

    void print() {
        cout << num << "/" << den << endl;
    }
};

int main() {
    Fraction f1(1, 2), f2(1, 4);
    Fraction f3 = f1 + f2;
    f3.print();
    Fraction f4 = f1 - f2;
    f4.print();
    Fraction f5 = f1 * f2;
    f5.print();

class rational{
    private:
    int numerator,denominator;
    public:
    rational(){
    };
    rational(int n,int d){
        numerator=n;
        denominator=d;
    }
    rational operator*(rational obj){
        rational t;
        t.numerator=numerator*obj.numerator;
        t.denominator=denominator*obj.denominator;
        return t;
    }
    rational operator/(rational obj){
        rational t;
        t.numerator=numerator*obj.denominator;
        t.denominator=denominator*obj.numerator;
        return t;
    }
    rational operator+(rational obj){
        rational t;
        t.numerator=(numerator*obj.denominator)+(obj.numerator*denominator);
        t.denominator=denominator*obj.denominator;
        return t;
    }
    rational operator-(rational obj){
        rational t;
        t.numerator=(numerator*obj.denominator)-(obj.numerator*denominator);
        t.denominator=denominator*obj.denominator;
        return t;
    }
    void display(){
        cout<<"the result is: "<<numerator<<" /"<<denominator<<endl;
    }
};

18/01/23, 09:09 - Viswaa Ramasubramanian: class Node:
    def __init__(self, datavalue=None):
        self.next = None
        self.datavalue = datavalue
        self.prev = None


class DoublyLinkedList:
    def __init__(self):
        self.head = None
        self.tail = None

    def insertAtHead(self, data):
        newnode = Node(data)
        newnode.next = self.head
        if self.head is not None:
            self.head.prev = newnode
        self.head = newnode
        if self.tail is None:
            self.tail = newnode

    def insertAtEnd(self, data):
        newnode = Node(data)
        if self.tail is not None:
            self.tail.next = newnode
            newnode.prev = self.tail
        self.tail = newnode
        if self.head is None:
            self.head = newnode

    def deleteAtHead(self):
        if self.head is None:
            return
        self.head = self.head.next
        if self.head is not None:
            self.head.prev = None

    def deleteAtEnd(self):
        if self.tail is None:
            return
        self.tail = self.tail.prev
        if self.tail is not None:
            self.tail.next = None

    def printForward(self):
        temp = self.head
        while temp:
            print(temp.datavalue, end=" ")
            temp = temp.next
        print()

    def printBackward(self):
        temp = self.tail
        while temp:
            print(temp.datavalue, end=" ")
            temp = temp.prev
        print()

    def deleteAll(self):
        self.head = None
        self.tail = None

18/01/23, 09:28 - Harecharan CSE E Amrita CBE: class Fraction:
    def __init__(self, n, d):
        self.num = n
        self.den = d

    # Overloading the + operator
    def __add__(self, f2):
        n = self.num * f2.den + self.den * f2.num
        d = self.den * f2.den
        return Fraction(n, d)

    # Overloading the - operator
    def __sub__(self, f2):
        n = self.num * f2.den - self.den * f2.num
        d = self.den * f2.den
        return Fraction(n, d)

    # Overloading the * operator
    def __mul__(self, f2):
        n = self.num * f2.num
        d = self.den * f2.den
        return Fraction(n, d)

    # Overloading the / operator
    def __truediv__(self, f2):
        n = self.num * f2.den
        d = self.den * f2.num
        return Fraction(n, d)

    # Overloading the < operator
    def __lt__(self, f2):
        return (self.num * f2.den < self.den * f2.num)

    def __str__(self):
        return str(self.num) + "/" + str(self.den)

f2 = Fraction(1, 4)

20/01/23, 01:08 - Harecharan CSE E Amrita CBE: In a database management system (DBMS), a sequence is a tool used to generate unique integers, typically used as a primary key for a table. Sequences are often used to generate unique values for primary keys when new rows are inserted into a table, without having to manually specify a value or use a complex key.

A sequence is created using the SQL statement "CREATE SEQUENCE", and the next value in the sequence can be retrieved using the "NEXT VALUE FOR" statement.

For example, to create a sequence called "employee_id_seq" that starts at 1 and increments by 1:

Copy code
CREATE SEQUENCE employee_id_seq START WITH 1 INCREMENT BY 1;
To use the sequence to generate a unique value when inserting a new row into the "employees" table:

Copy code
INSERT INTO employees (employee_id, first_name, last_name, salary)
VALUES (NEXT VALUE FOR employee_id_seq, 'John', 'Doe', 50000);
The above statement will insert a new row into the "employees" table, with a unique value for the "employee_id" column, generated from the "employee_id_seq" sequence.

Sequences can also have options like MINVALUE and MAXVALUE for the minimum and maximum value of the sequence, CYCLE option for cycling the sequence once it reaches the max value and CACHE option for caching a number of values for better performance.

It is important to note that sequences are not supported by all DBMS and the syntax for creating and using sequences may vary depending on the specific DBMS you are using.
